success\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         111 days, 1 hour, 49 minutes\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         90%\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         The clock was held at T-5 minutes to allow time to resolve a computer issue at the\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Range_Safety_Officer" title="Range Safety Officer">\n          Range Safety Officer\n         </a>\n         \'s console. The issue was resolved and the clock restarted in time to allow\n         <i>\n          Discovery\n         </i>\n         to launch with just two seconds left in the\n         <a href="/wiki/Launch_window" title="Launch window">\n          launch window\n         </a>\n         .\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-59">\n          <a href="#cite_note-59">\n           [59]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n         <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-60">\n          <a href="#cite_note-60">\n           [60]\n          </a>\n         </sup>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mission_timeline">\n        Mission timeline\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-133&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Mission timeline">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <dl>\n       <dd>\n        <i>\n         Section source: NASA Press Kit\n        </i>\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-61">\n         <a href="#cite_note-61">\n          [61]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n        and NASA TV Live\n        <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasalive_2-1">\n         <a href="#cite_note-nasalive-2">\n          [2]\n         </a>\n        </sup>\n        The original nominal mission of twelve days was eventually extended by two days, one at a time.\n       </dd>\n      </dl>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="24_February_(Flight_Day_1_\xe2\x80\x93_Launch)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="24_February_.28Flight_Day_1_.E2.80.93_Launch.29">\n        24 February (Flight Day 1 \xe2\x80\x93 Launch)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-133&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: 24 February (Flight Day 1 \xe2\x80\x93 Launch)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Space Shuttle\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       successfully lifted off from\n       <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center" title="Kennedy Space Center">\n        Kennedy Space Center\n       </a>\n       \'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center_Launch_Complex_39" title="Kennedy Space Center Launch Complex 39">\n        Launch Pad 39A\n       </a>\n       at 16:53:24 EST on 24 February 2011. Liftoff was initially set for 16:50:24, but was delayed for 3 minutes by a minor glitch in a computer system used by the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Range_Safety_Officer" title="Range Safety Officer">\n        Range Safety Officer\n       </a>\n       (RSO) for the\n       <a href="/wiki/Eastern_Range" title="Eastern Range">\n        Eastern Range\n       </a>\n       . Once\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       was cleared for launch, it took 8 minutes and 34 seconds to reach orbit. At approximately four minutes into flight, a piece of foam was seen breaking away from the External Tank. This foam was deemed not to be a threat, since it was liberated after the shuttle had left Earth\'s atmosphere. During\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       \'s ascent, NASA managers also reported that they saw three more additional instances of foam liberation.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-62">\n        <a href="#cite_note-62">\n         [62]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       These losses also occurred after aerodynamic sensitive times when debris could seriously damage the shuttle, and so were deemed non-threatening. NASA\'s engineers accounted the foam losses to a condition called "cryo-pumping". When the external tank is loaded with liquid hydrogen, the air trapped in the foam first liquifies. During the ride into orbit, as the hydrogen level in the tank drops, it warms up and the liquefied air turns back into a gas. The pressure generated due to the state change of hydrogen can cause parts of foam in the tank to come off.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-63">\n        <a href="#cite_note-63">\n         [63]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       Once on orbit, the crew of STS-133 opened the payload bay doors and activated the K\n       <sub>\n        u\n       </sub>\n       band antenna for high-speed communications with Mission Control. While the K\n       <sub>\n        u\n       </sub>\n       band antenna was being activated, Alvin Drew and Pilot Eric Boe activated the Shuttle Remote Manipulator System (SRMS), also known as the\n       <a href="/wiki/Canadarm" title="Canadarm">\n        Canadarm\n       </a>\n       . Later in the day, imagery of the External Tank during launch was downlinked for analysis.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NSFFD1_64-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NSFFD1-64">\n         [64]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:15px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-133_launch.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="3000" data-file-width="2000" height="120" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/STS-133_launch.jpg/80px-STS-133_launch.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/STS-133_launch.jpg/120px-STS-133_launch.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/07/STS-133_launch.jpg/160px-STS-133_launch.jpg 2x" width="80"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Space Shuttle\n           <i>\n            Discovery\n           </i>\n           rockets into orbit for the final time, 24 February 2011.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:41px auto;">\n           <div class="PopUpMediaTransform" id="mwe_player_0" style="width:120px;" videopayload=\'&lt;div class="mediaContainer" style="width:512px"&gt;&lt;video    <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35.5px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-133_Discovery_Lift_Off_Launch_Pad_39A_KSC.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="1985" data-file-width="3000" height="79" //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/9/9e/STS-133_Discovery_Lift_Off_Launch_Pad_39A_KSC.jpg/240px-STS-133_Discovery_Lift_Off_Launch_Pad_39A_KSC.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           <i>\n            Discovery\n           </i>\n           lifts off from Launch Pad 39A.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:41px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS133_launch.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="1080" data-file-width="1920" height="68" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/STS133_launch.jpg/120px-STS133_launch.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/STS133_launch.jpg/180px-STS133_launch.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0e/STS133_launch.jpg/240px-STS133_launch.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Close up of the launch from Pad 39A.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="25_February_(Flight_Day_2_\xe2\x80\x93_OBSS_inspection)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="25_February_.28Flight_Day_2_.E2.80.93_OBSS_inspection.29">\n        25 February (Flight Day 2 \xe2\x80\x93 OBSS inspection)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-133&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: 25 February (Flight Day 2 \xe2\x80\x93 OBSS inspection)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Flight Day 2 saw the crew of\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       begin their preparations to dock with the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n        International Space Station\n       </a>\n       (ISS). The day started with a firing of the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Orbital_Maneuvering_System" title="Orbital Maneuvering System">\n        Orbital Maneuvering System\n       </a>\n       (OMS) engine, called the NC2 burn, to help\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       catch up to the ISS. Commander Steve Lindsey, Pilot Eric Boe and Mission Specialist Al Drew began the day performing an inspection of the Re-enforced Carbon-Carbon (RCC) panels with the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Orbital_Boom_Sensor_System" title="Orbital Boom Sensor System">\n        Orbital Boom Sensor System\n       </a>\n       (OBSS). Lindsey and Boe started the inspection on the starboard wing and nose cap, and continued on with the port wing; the whole survey took about six hours to complete. Drew joined up with Michael Barratt and Steve Bowen to checkout and get their two\n       <a href="/wiki/Extravehicular_Mobility_Unit" title="Extravehicular Mobility Unit">\n        Extravehicular Mobility Units\n       </a>\n       (EMUs) ready for the two spacewalks that would be conducted during the mission. Later in the day, the crew checked out the rendezvous tools to ensure they were operational. At the end of the day, another OMS engine firing, known as the NC3 burn, took place.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NSFFD02_65-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NSFFD02-65">\n         [65]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="26_February_(Flight_Day_3_\xe2\x80\x93_ISS_rendezvous)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="26_February_.28Flight_Day_3_.E2.80.93_ISS_rendezvous.29">\n        26 February (Flight Day 3 \xe2\x80\x93 ISS rendezvous)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-133&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: 26 February (Flight Day 3 \xe2\x80\x93 ISS rendezvous)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       The orbiter docked to the ISS on Flight Day 3, marking the 13th time\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       had visited the ISS. The docking occurred on time at 19:14\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/UTC" title="UTC">\n        UTC\n       </a>\n       . A hard mate between the two vehicles was delayed by about 40 minutes because of relative motion between the station and shuttle, thus putting the crew behind the timeline for the day. The hatches were finally opened at 21:16 UTC, and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Expedition_26" title="Expedition 26">\n        Expedition 26\n       </a>\n       crew greeted the crew of STS-133.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-mccstat5_66-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-mccstat5-66">\n         [66]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       After the welcome ceremony and safety briefing, the crew\'s main task of the day was to transfer the\n       <a href="/wiki/ExPRESS_Logistics_Carrier" title="ExPRESS Logistics Carrier">\n        ExPRESS Logistics Carrier\n       </a>\n       4 (ELC-4). ELC-4 was taken out of\n       <i>\n        Discovery\'s\n       </i>\n       payload bay by the Space Station Remote Manipulator (SSRMS), also known as\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Canadarm2" title="Canadarm2">\n        Canadarm2\n       </a>\n       , which was operated by Nicole Stott and Michael Barratt. The SSRMS handed it to the Shuttle Remote Manipulator System (SRMS), which was being controlled by Boe and Drew, while the SSRMS moved to the Mobile Base System (MBS). Once there, the SSRMS took ELC-4 back from the SRMS, and installed it at its location on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Integrated_Truss_Structure" title="Integrated Truss Structure">\n        S3 truss\n       </a>\n       location. ELC-4 was installed in its final location at 03:22 UTC on 27 February.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfnfd3_67-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfnfd3-67">\n         [67]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       While the robotic transfer was going on, Bowen and Lindsey were transferring items that were needed for Flight Day 4 and the spacewalk on Flight Day 5.\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:30px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-133_Discovery_Nose_Forward_Underside_%26_Crew_Cabin.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2748" data-file-width="3664" height="90"        </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           View of the nose, the forward underside and crew cabin of\n           <i>\n          </a>\n           .\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-133_Discovery_seen_from_the_Cupola.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2832" data-file-width="4256"       </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           The docked\n           <i>\n            Discovery\n           </i>\n           and Dextre are featured in this photograph.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="27_February_(Flight_Day_4)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="27_February_.28Flight_Day_4.29">\n        27 February (Flight Day 4)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-133&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: 27 February (Flight Day 4)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       On Flight Day 4, Stott and Barratt grappled the\n       <a href="/wiki/Orbiter_Boom_Sensor_System" title="Orbiter Boom Sensor System">\n        Orbiter Boom Sensor System\n       </a>\n       (OBSS) using the Canadarm2 and removed it from the starboard sill of\n       <i>\n        Discovery\'s\n       </i>\n       payload bay. Once it was grappled and out of the payload bay, the Shuttle Remote Manipulator System grappled the end of the OBSS and took a hand off from the Canadarm2. The OBSS was grappled by the space station arm, because the SRMS could not reach it due to clearance issues, and it needed to be moved out of the way so that the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Permanent_Multipurpose_Module" title="Permanent Multipurpose Module">\n        Permanent Multipurpose Module\n       </a>\n       (PMM) could be removed from the payload bay. After the OBSS hand off, the entire STS-133 crew was joined by ISS\n       <a href="/wiki/Expedition_26" title="Expedition 26">\n        Expedition 26\n       </a>\n       commander\n       <a href="/wiki/Scott_Kelly_(astronaut)" title="Scott Kelly (astronaut)">\n        Scott Kelly\n       </a>\n       and flight engineer\n       <a href="/wiki/Paolo_Nespoli" title="Paolo Nespoli">\n        Paolo Nespoli\n       </a>\n       for a series of in-flight media interviews. The interviews were conducted with the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Weather_Channel" title="Weather Channel">\n        Weather Channel\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/WBZ_(AM)" title="WBZ (AM)">\n        WBZ\n       </a>\n       radio in\n       <a href="/wiki/Boston" title="Boston">\n        Boston, Massachusetts\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/WSB-TV" title="WSB-TV">\n        WSB-TV\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Atlanta" title="Atlanta">\n        Atlanta, Georgia\n       </a>\n       , and\n       <a href="/wiki/WBTV" title="WBTV">\n        WBTV\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Charlotte,_North_Carolina" title="Charlotte, North Carolina">\n        Charlotte, North Carolina\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-mccstat7_68-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-mccstat7-68">\n         [68]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The crew also completed more cargo transfers to and from the ISS. Throughout the day, Drew and Bowen prepared tools that they would use on their spacewalk on Flight Day 5. Later in the day, they were joined by the shuttle crew and ISS commander Kelly and Flight Engineer Nespoli, for a review of the spacewalk procedures. After the review, Bowen and Drew donned oxygen masks and entered the crew lock of the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Quest_airlock" title="Quest airlock">\n        Quest airlock\n       </a>\n       for the standard pre-spacewalk campout. The airlock was lowered to 10.2 psi for the night. This was done to help the spacewalkers purge\n       <a href="/wiki/Nitrogen" title="Nitrogen">\n        nitrogen\n       </a>\n       from their blood and help prevent\n       <a href="/wiki/Decompression_sickness" title="Decompression sickness">\n        decompression sickness\n       </a>\n       , also known as the bends.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sfnfd4_69-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sfnfd4-69">\n         [69]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="28_February_(Flight_Day_5_\xe2\x80\x93_EVA_1)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="28_February_.28Flight_Day_5_.E2.80.93_EVA_1.29">\n        28 February (Flight Day 5 \xe2\x80\x93 EVA 1)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-133&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: 28 February (Flight Day 5 \xe2\x80\x93 EVA 1)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <p>\n       Steve Bowen and Alvin Drew performed the mission\'s first\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Extra-vehicular_activity" title="Extra-vehicular activity">\n        extra-vehicular activity\n       </a>\n       (EVA), or spacewalk, on Flight Day 5. After waking up at 6:23\xc2\xa0am EST, the crew immediately began EVA preparations.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-eva1_70-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-eva1-70">\n         [70]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       A conference was held between the crew of the station and Mission Control at about 8:20\xc2\xa0am, followed by further EVA preparation work, including the depressurization of the airlock. Bowen and Drew switched their spacesuits to internal battery power at 10:46\xc2\xa0am, marking the beginning of EVA 1.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-eva1_70-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-eva1-70">\n         [70]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       During the EVA, Bowen and Drew installed a power cable linking the\n       <i>\n        Unity\n       </i>\n       and\n       <i>\n        Tranquility\n       </i>\n       modules in order to provide a contingency power source, should it become required. They then moved a failed ammonia pump, which was replaced in August 2010, from its temporary location to the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/External_Stowage_Platform" title="External Stowage Platform">\n        External Stowage Platform 2\n       </a>\n       . Later, operations with the SSRMS robotic arm were delayed to due technical problems with the robotic control station in the\n       <i>\n        Cupola\n       </i>\n       module.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-eva1_70-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-eva1-70">\n         [70]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       After installing a wedge under a camera on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Integrated_Truss_Structure" title="Integrated Truss Structure">\n        S3 truss\n       </a>\n       to provide clearance from the newly installed\n       <a href="/wiki/ExPRESS_Logistics_Carrier" title="ExPRESS Logistics Carrier">\n        ExPRESS Logistics Carrier\n       </a>\n       -2, performing a Japanese experiment called\n       <i>\n        Message in a Bottle\n       </i>\n       to collect a sample of vacuum, and other minor tasks, the EVA ended after six hours and 34 minutes at 5:20\xc2\xa0pm EST.\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:STS-133_Bowen_%26_Drew_Spacewalk.jpg">\n            <img alt="" data-file-height="2848" data-file-width="4288" height="80" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/STS-133_Bowen_%26_Drew_Spacewalk.jpg/120px-STS-133_Bowen_%26_Drew_Spacewalk.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/STS-133_Bowen_%26_Drew_Spacewalk.jpg/180px-STS-133_Bowen_%26_Drew_Spacewalk.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7a/STS-133_Bowen_%26_Drew_Spacewalk.jpg/240px-STS-133_Bowen_%26_Drew_Spacewalk.jpg 2x" width="120"/>\n           </a>\n          </div>\n         </div>\n         <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Bowen &amp; Drew (partially obscured at centre) during EVA 1.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a    <div class="gallerytext">\n          <p>\n           Bowen &amp; Drew during EVA 1.\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="1_March_(Flight_Day_6_\xe2\x80\x93_PMM_installation)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="1_March_.28Flight_Day_6_.E2.80.93_PMM_installation.29">\n        1 March (Flight Day 6 \xe2\x80\x93 PMM installation)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-133&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: 1 March (Flight Day 6 \xe2\x80\x93 PMM installation)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox mbox-small-left ambox-content" role="presentation">\n       <tr>\n        <td class="mbox-image">\n         <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg">\n          <img alt="[icon]" data-file-height="31" data-file-width="44" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/20px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/30px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/40px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 2x" width="20"/>\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td class="mbox-text">\n         <div class="mbox-text-span">\n          <b>\n           This section needs expansion\n          </b>\n          .\n          <small>\n           You can help by\n           <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=STS-133&amp;action=edit&amp;section=">\n            adding to it\n           </a>\n           .\n          </small>\n          <small>\n           <i>\n            (May 2011)\n           </i>\n          </small>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Flight Day 6 saw the installation of the\n       <i>\n        Leonardo\n       </i>\n       Permanent Multipurpose Module (PMM) to the nadir, or Earth-facing, port of the station\'s\n       <i>\n        Unity\n       </i>\n       module. Once the installation was complete, the external outfitting of\n       <i>\n        Leonardo\n       </i>\n       , to integrate it into the ISS as a permanent module, was begun. Bowen and Drew conducted the procedure review for the mission\'s second spacewalk, before beginning their pre-EVA campout in the Quest airlock.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="2_March_(Flight_Day_7_\xe2\x80\x93_EVA_2)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="2_March_.28Flight_Day_7_.E2.80.93_EVA_2.29">\n        2 March (Flight Day 7 \xe2\x80\x93 EVA 2)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-133&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: 2 March (Flight Day 7 \xe2\x80\x93 EVA 2)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox mbox-small-left ambox-content" role="presentation">\n       <tr>\n        <td class="mbox-image">\n         <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg">\n          <img alt="[icon]" data-file-height="31" data-file-width="44" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/20px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/30px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/40px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 2x" width="20"/>\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td class="mbox-text">\n         <div class="mbox-text-span">\n          <b>\n           This section needs expansion\n          </b>\n          .\n          <small>\n           You can help by\n           <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=STS-133&amp;action=edit&amp;section=">\n            adding to it\n           </a>\n           .\n          </small>\n          <small>\n           <i>\n            (May 2011)\n           </i>\n          </small>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       Bowen and Drew conducted STS-133\'s second EVA on Flight Day 7. Drew removed thermal insulation from a platform, while Bowen swapped out an attachment bracket on the\n       <i>\n        Columbus\n       </i>\n       module. Bowen then installed a camera assembly on the\n       <a href="/wiki/Dextre" title="Dextre">\n        Dextre\n       </a>\n       robot and removed insulation from Dextre\'s electronics platform. Drew installed a light on a cargo cart and repaired some dislodged thermal insulation from a valve on the truss. Meanwhile, the ISS and shuttle crew entered the\n       <i>\n        Leonardo\n       </i>\n       PMM to commence the internal outfitting of the module.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="3_March_(Flight_Day_8)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="3_March_.28Flight_Day_8.29">\n        3 March (Flight Day 8)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-133&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: 3 March (Flight Day 8)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox mbox-small-left ambox-content" role="presentation">\n       <tr>\n        <td class="mbox-image">\n         <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg">\n          <img alt="[icon]"       (May 2011)\n           </i>\n          </small>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       On Flight Day 8, the transfer of the\n       <i>\n        Leonardo\n       </i>\n       PMM\'s cargo to the interior of the ISS began. The crew also received some off-duty time on this day.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="4_March_(Flight_Day_9)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="4_March_.28Flight_Day_9.29">\n        4 March (Flight Day 9)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-133&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: 4 March (Flight Day 9)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox mbox-small-left ambox-content" role="presentation">\n       <tr>\n        <td class="mbox-image">\n         <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg">\n          <img alt="[icon]" data-file-height="31" data-file-width="44" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/20px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/30px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/40px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 2x" width="20"/>\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td class="mbox-text">\n         <div class="mbox-text-span">\n          <b>\n           This section needs expansion\n          </b>\n          .\n          <small>\n           You can help by\n           <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=STS-133&amp;action=edit&amp;section=">\n            adding to it\n           </a>\n           .\n          </small>\n          <small>\n           <i>\n            (May 2011)\n           </i>\n          </small>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       On Flight Day 9, the equipment used on Drew and Bowen\'s spacewalk was reconfigured. A joint crew news conference was also conducted via satellite, after which the crew received more off-duty time.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="5_March_(Flight_Day_10)">\n       </span>\n    </i>\n       PMM continued on Flight Day 10.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-mission_extension_71-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-mission_extension-71">\n         [71]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Furthermore, a photo shoot of the ISS with multiple spacecraft docked was considered, but rejected by mission planners.\n       <sup class="reference"       (May 2011)\n           </i>\n          </small>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       As well as the continued outfitting of the\n       <i>\n        Leonardo\n       </i>\n       Permanent Multipurpose Module,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-mission_extension_71-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-mission_extension-71">\n         [71]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       a checkout of\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       \'s rendezvous tools was conducted on Flight Day 11, before the shuttle crew said their farewells to the ISS crew, exited the station and sealed the hatch between the orbiter and the ISS. The installation of a center-line camera was also conducted on this day.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="7_March_(Flight_Day_12_\xe2\x80\x93_Undocking)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="7_March_.28Flight_Day_12_.E2.80.93_Undocking.29">\n        7 March (Flight Day 12 \xe2\x80\x93 Undocking)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span       (May 2011)\n           </i>\n          </small>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       conducted its final undocking from the ISS on Flight Day 12, and its last fly-around preceded the final separation from the station. A late inspection of\n       <i>\n        Discovery\'\n       </i>\n       s\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Thermal_Protection_System" title="Thermal Protection System">\n        Thermal Protection System\n       </a>\n       was conducted using the\n       <a href="/wiki/Orbiter_Boom_Sensor_System" title="Orbiter Boom Sensor System">\n        OBSS\n       </a>\n       , before the OBSS was berthed.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="8_March_(Flight_Day_13)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="8_March_.28Flight_Day_13.29">\n        8 March (Flight Day 13)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-133&amp;action=edit&amp;section=31" title="Edit section: 8 March (Flight Day 13)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox mbox-small-left ambox-content" role="presentation">\n       <tr>\n        <td class="mbox-image">\n  <div class="mbox-text-span">\n          <b>\n           This section needs expansion\n          </b>\n          .\n          <small>\n           You can help by\n           <a class="external text" stowed their equipment in the sle\'s cabin before conducting a checkout of the flight control system and a hot-fire test of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Reaction_control_system" title="Reaction control system">\n        reaction control system\n       </a>\n       . A final deorbit preparation briefing was carried out before the shuttle\'s K\n       <sub>\n        u\n       </sub>\n       band antenna was stowed.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span id="9_March_(Flight_Day_14_\xe2\x80\x93_Re-entry_and_landing)">\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="9_March_.28Flight_Day_14_.E2.80.93_Re-entry_and_landing.29">\n        9 March (Flight Day 14 \xe2\x80\x93 Re-entry and landing)\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-133&amp;action=edit&amp;section=32" title="Edit section: 9 March (Flight Day 14 \xe2\x80\x93 Re-entry and landing)">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <table class="plainlinks metadata ambox mbox-small-left ambox-content" role="presentation">\n       <tr>\n        <td class="mbox-image">\n         <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg">\n          <img alt="[icon]" data-file-height="31" data-file-width="44" height="14" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/20px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/30px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg/40px-Wiki_letter_w_cropped.svg.png 2x" width="20"/>\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td class="mbox-text">\n         <div class="mbox-text-span">\n          <b>\n           This section needs expansion\n          </b>\n          .\n          <small>\n           You can help by\n           <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=STS-133&amp;action=edit&amp;section=">\n            adding to it\n           </a>\n           .\n          </small>\n          <small>\n           <i>\n            (May 2011)\n           </i>\n          </small>\n         </div>\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <p>\n       On the final day of the mission,\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       \'s crew carried out further deorbit preparations, and closed the shuttle\'s payload bay doors. A successful deorbit burn and re-entry ended with\n       <i>\n        Discovery\n       </i>\n       landing at\n       <a href="/wiki/Kennedy_Space_Center" title="Kennedy Space Center">\n        Kennedy Space Center\n       </a>\n       \'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Shuttle_Landing_Facility" title="Shuttle Landing Facility">\n        Shuttle Landing Facility\n       </a>\n       for the final time on 9 March 2011 at 11:58:14 EST. The shuttle was retired at wheel-stop.\n      </p>\n      <ul class="gallery mw-gallery-traditional center">\n       <li class="gallerybox" style="width: 155px">\n        <div style="width: 155px">\n         <div class="thumb" style="width: 150px;">\n          <div style="margin:35px auto;">\n           <a class="image"  Video recording of the STS-133 landing.\n           <br/>\n           (2 mins 30 secs)\n          </p>\n         </div>\n        </div>\n       </li>\n      </ul>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Spacewalks">\n        Spacewalks\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-133&amp;action=edit&amp;section=33" title="Edit section: Spacewalks">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       Two spacewalks (EVAs) were conducted during the mission.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-STS_133_duration_and_eva_73-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-STS_133_duration_and_eva-73">\n         [73]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <table class="wikitable">\n       <tr>\n        <th style="width: 5em;">\n         EVA\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Spacewalkers\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Start (\n         <a href="/wiki/Coordinated_Universal_Time" title="Coordinated Universal Time">\n          UTC\n         </a>\n         )\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         End (UTC)\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Duration\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td rowspan="2">\n         EVA 1\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Stephen_G._Bowen" title="Stephen G. Bowen">\n          Steve Bowen\n         </a>\n         <br/>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Benjamin_Alvin_Drew" title="Benjamin Alvin Drew">\n          Alvin Drew\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         28 February 2011\n         <br/>\n         15:46\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         28 February 2011\n         <br/>\n         22:20\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         6 hours 34 minutes\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="4">\n         Drew and Bowen installed a power extension cable between the Unity and Tranquility nodes to provide a contingency power source should it be required. The spacewalkers then moved the failed ammonia pump module that was replaced in August from its temporary location to the\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/External_Stowage_Platform" title="External Stowage Platform">\n          External Stowage Platform 2\n         </a>\n         adjacent to the\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Quest_airlock" title="Quest airlock">\n          Quest airlock\n         </a>\n         . Drew and Bowen then installed a wedge under a camera on the\n         <a href="/wiki/Integrated_Truss_Structure" title="Integrated Truss Structure">\n          S3 truss\n         </a>\n         to provide clearance from the newly installed ELC-4. They next replaced a guide for the rail cart system used for moving the station robotic arm along the truss. The guides had been removed when astronauts were performing work on the station\'s starboard\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Solar_Alpha_Rotary_Joint" title="Solar Alpha Rotary Joint">\n          Solar Alpha Rotary Joint\n         </a>\n         (SARJ), which rotates the solar arrays to track the sun. The final task was to "fill" a special bottle with the vacuum of space for a Japanese education payload. The bottle will be part of a public museum exhibit.\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td rowspan="2">\n         EVA 2\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         Steve Bowen\n         <br/>\n         Alvin Drew\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         2 March 2011\n         <br/>\n         15:42\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         2 March 2011\n         <br/>\n         21:56\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         6 hours 14 minutes\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td colspan="4">\n         Drew removed thermal insulation from a platform, while Bowen swapped out an attachment bracket on the\n         <a href="/wiki/Columbus_(ISS_module)" title="Columbus (ISS module)">\n          <i>\n           Columbus\n          </i>\n          module\n         </a>\n         . Bowen then installed a camera assembly on the\n         <a href="/wiki/Dextre" title="Dextre">\n          Dextre\n         </a>\n         robot and removed insulation from Dextre\'s electronics platform. Drew installed a light on a cargo cart and repaired some dislodged thermal insulation from a valve on the truss.\n        </td>\n       </tr>\n      </table>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Wake-up_calls">\n        Wake-up calls\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=STS-133&amp;action=edit&amp;section=34" title="Edit section: Wake-up calls">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       NASA began a tradition of playing music to astronauts during the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gemini_program" title="Gemini program">\n        Gemini program\n       </a>\n       , and first used music to wake up a flight crew during\n       <a href="/wiki/Apollo_15" title="Apollo 15">\n        Apollo 15\n       </a>\n       . Each track is specially chosen, often by the astronauts\' families, and usually has a special meaning to an individual member of the crew, or is applicable to their daily activities.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-chronology_74-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-chronology-74">\n         [74]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-wakeup_75-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-wakeup-75">\n         [75]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       NASA opened the selection process to the public for the first time for STS-133. The public was invited to vote on two songs used to wake up astronauts on previous missions to wake up the STS-133 crew.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-76">\n        <a href="#cite_note-76">\n         [76]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <table class="wikitable">\n       <tr>\n        <th>\n         Flight Day\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Song\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Artist\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Played for\n        </th>\n        <th>\n         Links\n        </th>\n       </tr>\n       <tr>\n        <td>\n         Day 2\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         "\n         <a href="/wiki/The_Prince_of_Egypt_(soundtrack)" title="The Prince of Egypt (soundtrack)">\n          Through Heaven\'s Eyes\n         </a>\n         "\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a href="/wiki/Brian_Stokes_Mitchell" title="Brian Stokes Mitchell">\n          Brian Stokes Mitchell\n         </a>\n        </td>\n        <td>\n         <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Michael_R._Barratt" title="Michael R. Barratt">\n          Michael R.
